LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b0].[Id], [b0].[BookingId], [b0].[Quantity], [b0].[TotalPrice], [s].[Id] AS [Id0], [s].[BookingDetailsId], [s].[CreatedAt], [s].[QRCode], [s].[TicketTypeId], [s].[TicketTypeId1], [s].[Used], [s].[UserId], [s].[Id0] AS [Id00], [s].[ConfirmedTickets], [s].[EventId], [s].[Name], [s].[Price], [s].[TotalTickets], [s].[Id1], [s].[CategoryId], [s].[CompanyId], [s].[Description], [s].[EndBookingTime], [s].[EndTime], [s].[Location], [s].[Sales], [s].[StartBookingTime], [s].[StartTime], [s].[Title]
